    function getWindowDimensions() {
        var width = window.innerWidth ||
            document.documentElement.clientWidth ||
            document.body.clientWidth;
        var height = window.innerHeight ||
            document.documentElement.clientHeight ||
            document.body.clientHeight;
        return [width, height];
    }
    function parseSizeMappings(sizeMappings) {

    $('#site-search-457704').on('submit', function(){
        // Filter query
        var sQueryFiltered = $("#site-search-457704 input[name=q]").val().replace(/\?/g, '');
    $("#site-search-457704 input[name=q]").val( sQueryFiltered );

        if( $('#site-search-457704-term').val() ){
            return true;
        }else{
            return false;
        }

               <script>
                jQuery(document).ready(function($){
                    var $form = $('#mailinglist-form-563345');
                    if( $form.length > 0 ){
                        $form.validate({
                            rules: {
                                "list_id[]": {
                                    required: true,
                                    minlength: 1
                                }
                            },
                            messages: {
                                'list_id[]': 'You must select at least one email list.'
                            },
                            errorPlacement: function(error, element){
                                error.appendTo( element.parents('.form-group') );
                            },
                            errorClass: 'has-error text-danger',
                            validClass: 'has-success text-success',
                            highlight: function(element, errorClass, validClass){
                                $(element).parents('.form-group').addClass(errorClass).removeClass(validClass);
                            },
                            unhighlight: function(element, errorClass, validClass){
                                $(element).parents('.form-group').removeClass(errorClass).addClass(validClass);
                            }
                        });
                    }

                    /* executes when all ajax requests have finished */
                    function mlist_finished($form){
                        $form.find('.mailinglist-save .tnt-svg').hide();
                        $form.find('.mailinglist-save').prop('disabled', false);
                        $form.find('.mailinglist-item input:checked').each(function(){
                            $(this).prop('checked',false);
                        });
                        $form.find('.form-group').removeClass('has-success text-success');
                        $form.find('.email').val('');
                    }

                    $form.submit(function(e) {
                        e.preventDefault();

                        var $success_alert = $form.parents('.email-signup').find('.alert-success');
                        var $error_alert = $form.parents('.email-signup').find('.alert-danger');
                        
                        if ($success_alert.is(':visible')) {
                            $success_alert.fadeOut(400);
                        }
                        
                        if ($error_alert.is(':visible')) {
                            $error_alert.fadeOut(400);
                        }

                        if( $form.valid() ){
                            $form.find('.mailinglist-save').prop('disabled', true);
                            $form.find('.mailinglist-save .tnt-svg').show();

                            $.ajax({
                                type: "POST",
                                url: $(this).attr('action'),
                                data: $(this).serialize(),
                                success: function(data){
                                    $success_alert
                                        .html('<p><strong>Success!</strong> An email has been sent to <strong>'+ data.email +'</strong> with a link to confirm list signup.</p>')
                                        .fadeIn(400, mlist_finished($form));
                                },
                                error: function(data){
                                    __tnt.log('Ajax was unsuccessful');
                                    $error_alert.fadeIn(400, mlist_finished($form));
                                }
                            });

                            
                        }
                    });
                });
               </script>

            <script>
             function getCookie(cname) {
    var name = cname + "=";
    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    for(var i=0; i<ca.length; i++){
      var c = ca[i].trim();
      if (c.indexOf(name)==0) return c.substring(name.length,c.length);
    }
    return "";
  }$(document).ready(function() {
    // Initialize the plugin
    $('#block-563345').popup();
    if (location.href.indexOf('article_')==-1){
      if (getCookie('sbtnletterPop')==''){
        
        var popupTimer = setTimeout(function(){ $('#block-563345').popup('show'); }, 10000);
          
        var nLetterDate = new Date();
        nLetterDate.setTime(nLetterDate.getTime() + (30*24*60*60*1000));
        var nLetterExp = "expires="+nLetterDate.toUTCString();
        document.cookie = "sbtnletterPop=1; " + nLetterExp + "; path=/";
      }
    }  
  });
            </script>

   __tnt.trackEvent = function(obj) {
            if( jQuery.type(obj) === 'object' ){
                
                    
                        
                        if(obj.category && obj.action){
                            __tnt.googleEvent(obj);
                        } else if(obj.network && obj.socialAction){
                            __tnt.googleSocial(obj);
                        } else if(obj.url){
                            __tnt.googlePageView(obj);
                        }
                    if(typeof TNCMS.Tracking != 'undefined' && obj.metric){
                        TNCMS.Tracking.addEvent({
                            app: obj.app,
                            metric: obj.metric,
                            id: obj.uuid
                        });
                    }
                
            }
        }
        
        if(__tnt.trackEventLater.length > 0){
            jQuery(__tnt.trackEventLater).each(function(){
                __tnt.trackEvent($(this));
            });
        }

            var trkObj = jQuery(this).data('track');

        });
